Yet, even after adding Fanboy's two extra lists, hpHosts’s Ad and tracking servers, uBlock Origin still has a lower memory footprint than other very popular blockers out there.\r\n\r\nAlso, be aware that selecting some of these extra lists may lead to higher likelihood of web site breakage -- especially those lists which are normally used as hosts file.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nFree.\r\nOpen source with public license (GPLv3)\r\nFor users by users.\r\n\r\nIf ever you really do want to contribute something, think about the people working hard to maintain the filter lists you are using, which were made available to use by all for free.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nDocumentation:\r\nhttps://github.com/gorhill/uBlock#ublock-origin\r\n\r\nProject change log:\r\nhttps://github.com/nikrolls/uBlock-Edge/releases\r\n\r\nContributors @ Github:\r\nhttps://github.com/nikrolls/uBlock-Edge/graphs/contributors\r\n\r\nContributors @ Crowdin:\r\nhttps://crowdin.net/project/ublock","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NBLGGH4RFHK","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"AdBlock","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.64693.13510798887413064.7dec4a64-65c8-45c3-96b8-8f8f9b2600a0.d2f3940c-9467-43d9-9cc5-448ef5148c5b","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"white","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"مجاني","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":4.0,"RatingsCount":"1","PackageFamilyNames":["BetaFish.AdBlock_c1wakc4j0nefm"],"ContentIds":["e56f1d49-7ed1-85c0-f549-2914e47e34b2"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"كمبيوتر شخصي","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"AdBlock.
